\BeginGroup\: BSA tricks
\----------

Better Cities .esp
? Dummy file to load Better Cities .BSA
BSAloader.esp
? Dummy file to load .BSA files.
FraNewItems.esp
? Dummy file to load FraNewItems.BSA
? Using a file to load a BSA means the BSA must NOT be listed in Oblivion.ini at the same time or the game will not load.
? This is ususally only a problem when automatic installers insert the name into Oblivion.ini then the user creates a BSA redirection file later.
Fra.esp
? BSA redirection hack. Usually refers to FraNewItems.BSA
? Using a file to load a BSA means the BSA must NOT be listed in Oblivion.ini at the same time or the game will not load.
? This is ususally only a problem when automatic installers insert the name into Oblivion.ini then the user creates a BSA redirection file later.
MMM.esp
? Dummy file to load the MMM .BSA.
Oblivion.esp
? Usually a BSA redirection hack.
? Using a file to load a BSA means the BSA must NOT be listed in Oblivion.ini at the same time or the game will not load.
? This is ususally only a problem when automatic installers insert the name into Oblivion.ini then the user creates a BSA redirection file later.
TamRes.esp
? Dummy file to load the TamRes BSA.
\EndGroup\\
